gfes_translations_strings

Outputs all of the translations strings for Gravity Forms.

Description

gfes_translations_strings(); 

Usage

  1. if ( !function_exists( 'gfes_translations_strings' ) ) { 
  2.     require_once ABSPATH . PLUGINDIR . 'gravity-forms-spanish/gravityforms.php'; 
  3. } 
  4.  
  5.   
  6. // NOTICE! Understand what this does before running. 
  7. $result = gfes_translations_strings(); 
  8.     

Defined (2)

The function is defined in the following location(s).

/gravityforms.php
